)\\n29: \\n30: // Periodic compacts the log by purging revisions older than\\n31: // the configured retention time.\\n32: type Periodic struct {\\n33: \\tlg     *zap.Logger\\n34: \\tclock  clockwork.Clock\\n35: \\tperiod time.Duration\\n36: \\n37: \\trg RevGetter\\n38: \\tc  Compactable\\n39: \\n40: \\trevs   []int64\\n41: \\tctx    context.Context\\n42: \\tcancel purges\\n50: // the log older than h Duration.\\n51: func newPeriodic(lg *zap.Logger, clock clockwork.Clock, h time.Duration, rg RevGetter, c Compactable) *Periodic {\\n52: \\tpc := &Periodic{\\n53: \\t\\tlg:     lg,\\n54: \\t\\tclock:  clock,\\n55: \\t\\tperiod: h,\\n56: \\t\\trg:     rg,\\n57: \\t\\tc:      c,\\n58: \\t}\\n59: \\t// revs won't be longer than the retentions.\\n60: \\tpc.revs = make([]int64, 0, pc.getRetentions())\\n61: \\tpc.ctx, pc.cancel = context.WithCancel(context.Background())\\n62: \\treturn pc\\n63: }\\n64: \\n65: /*\\n66: Compaction period 1-hour:\\n67:   1. compute compaction period, which is 1-hour\\n68:   2. record revisions for every 1/10 of 1-hour (6-minute)\\n69:   3. keep recording revisions with no compaction for first 1-hour\\n70:   4. do compact with revs[0]\\n71: \\t- success? continue on for-loop and move sliding window; revs = revs[1:]\\n72: \\t- failure? update revs, and retry after 1/10 of 1-hour (6-minute)\\n73: \\n74: Compaction period 24-hour:\\n75:   1. compute compaction period, which is 24-hour\\n76:   2. record revisions for every 1/10 of 24-hour (144-minute)\\n77:   3. keep recording revisions with no compaction for first 24-hour\\n78:   4. do compact with revs[0]\\n79: \\t- success? continue on for-loop and move sliding window; revs = revs[1:]\\n80: \\t- failure? update revs, and retry after 1/10 of 24-hour (Multi-Version Concurrency Control) compaction involves periodic cleanup of old revisions and intelligent management of watch streams that span compacted revisions. The following describes the key components:\\n\\n### 1. Compaction Scheduling: Periodic vs Revision-based\\n\\nCompaction is scheduled through two modes configured via `--auto-compaction-mode`:\\n\\n**Periodic Compaction** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/periodic.go:Periodic`):\\n- Records revisions periodically (every 1/10th of the retention period)\\n- Executes compaction after the retention period has elapsed\\n- For retention periods < 1 hour: compacts every X hours (e.g., 10m retention → compact every 10m)\\n- For retention periods ≥ 1 hour: compacts every 1 hour\\n- Implements exponential backoff retry on failure (lines 100-163)\\n\\n**Revision-based Compaction** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/revision.go:Revision`):\\n- Compacts at a fixed interval (5 minutes via `revInterval`)\\n- Retains a specified number of revisions from the current maximum revision\\n- Calculates: `compactionRev = currentRev - retention` (lines 64-112)\\n\\nBoth implementations are created through the factory pattern in `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/compactor.go:New()` (lines 55-73), which routes to either periodic or revision-based compaction.\\n\\n### 2. Compaction of Revision Indices\\n\\n**Index Compaction** (`server/storage/mvcc/key_index.go`):\\n- The `Compact()` method on `keyIndex` removes old revisions of keys\\n- Processes the `generations` structure (lines 44-72 in key_index.go comments) which tracks key mutations\\n- `doCompact()` (lines 258-282) walks through key generations and removes revisions <= compactionRev\\n- Maintains `available` map to track which revisions should be kept\\n\\n**Backend Compaction** (`server/storage/mvcc/kvstore_compaction.go:scheduleCompaction`):\\n- Iterates through backend storage in batches (lines 42-99)\\n- Deletes entries with revisions that are not in the `keep` map (generated from index compaction)\\n- Uses configurable batch limits via `CompactionBatchLimit` and sleep intervals via `CompactionSleepInterval`\\n- Records metrics: `indexCompactionPauseMs`, `dbCompactionTotalMs`, `dbCompactionKeysCounter`, `dbCompactionLast`\\n\\n### 3. Notification of Watch Streams Spanning Compacted Revisions\\n\\nWhen a watcher's minimum revision falls below the compaction revision, it must be notified:\\n\\n**Watch Stream Cancellation** (`server/storage/mvcc/watcher_group.go:chooseAll`, lines 237-266):\\n- During sync of unsynced watchers, `chooseAll()` checks if `w.minRev < compactRev`\\n- Sends a `WatchResponse` with `CompactRevision: compactRev` (line 253)\\n- Marks the watcher as `compacted = true` (line 254)\\n- Removes the watcher from the group (line 255)\\n- This notification tells clients their watch window has been compacted away\\n\\n**Watch Synchronization** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go:syncWatchers`, lines 346-414):\\n- Unsynced watchers are synced in batches (maxWatchersPerSync = 512)\\n- Retrieves events from current store state and sends to watchers\\n- Watches that couldn't send due to full channels become \\\"victims\\\" (lines 390-405)\\n- Calls `slowWatcherGauge.Set()` to track slow watchers (line 411)\\n\\n**Victim Handling** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go:moveVictims` and `syncVictimsLoop`, lines 257-339):\\n- Maintains a list of blocked watchers (\\\"victims\\\") that couldn't receive events\\n- Retries sending events to victims every 10ms (line 272)\\n- Once successfully sent, moves watchers back to synced/unsynced groups\\n- Decrements `slowWatcherGauge` when a slow watcher is no longer slow (line 324)\\n\\n### 4. Slow Watch Detection\\n\\nSlow watchers (watchers that fall behind) are tracked and managed:\\n\\n**Metrics** (`server/storage/mvcc/metrics.go`):\\n- `slowWatcherGauge` (lines 87-94): Tracks total number of unsynced slow watchers\\n- `pendingEventsGauge` (lines 105-112): Tracks pending events awaiting delivery\\n- Updated during `syncWatchers()` at line 411 of watchable_store.go\\n\\n**Detection Mechanism** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go`):\\n- When a watcher's channel is full (can't send), it's marked as `victim = true` (line 505)\\n- The slow watcher gauge is incremented (line 508) when moved to unsynced\\n- The gauge is decremented (line 324) when the watcher recovers\\n- Slow watchers are defined as unsynced watchers that haven't caught up to current revision\\n\\n### 5. Integration with Server\\n\\nThe compactor is integrated into the etcd server (`server/etcdserver/server.go`):\\n- Field `compactor v3compactor.Compactor` (line 266) holds the active compactor\\n- Created during server startup with `v3compactor.New()` \\n- Runs in a background goroutine via `srv.compactor.Run()` (line 388)\\n- Stopped via `compactor.Stop()` during graceful shutdown (line 962)\\n\\n### Key Files Summary\\n\\n1. **Compaction Scheduling**: `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/{compactor.go, periodic.go, revision.go}`\\n2. **Compaction Implementation**: `server/storage/mvcc/{kvstore_compaction.go, key_index.go}`\\n3. **Watch Stream Management**: `server/storage/mvcc/{watchable_store.go, watcher_group.go, watcher.go}`\\n4. **Metrics and Monitoring**: `server/storage/mvcc/metrics.go`\\n5. **Server Integration**: `server/etcdserver/server.go`\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3160,"cache_read_input_tokens":111270,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3160},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"15fcf7d8-cd4a-4769-ad6a-609795b88fe3","uuid":"e80eaf57-1c70-4ad1-bb3b-ef1a5c241df5"}

(Multi-Version Concurrency Control) compaction involves periodic cleanup of old revisions and intelligent management of watch streams that span compacted revisions. The following describes the key components:\\n\\n### 1. Compaction Scheduling: Periodic vs Revision-based\\n\\nCompaction is scheduled through two modes configured via `--auto-compaction-mode`:\\n\\n**Periodic Compaction** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/periodic.go:Periodic`):\\n- Records revisions periodically (every 1/10th of the retention period)\\n- Executes compaction after the retention period has elapsed\\n- For retention periods < 1 hour: compacts every X hours (e.g., 10m retention → compact every 10m)\\n- For retention periods ≥ 1 hour: compacts every 1 hour\\n- Implements exponential backoff retry on failure (lines 100-163)\\n\\n**Revision-based Compaction** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/revision.go:Revision`):\\n- Compacts at a fixed interval (5 minutes via `revInterval`)\\n- Retains a specified number of revisions from the current maximum revision\\n- Calculates: `compactionRev = currentRev - retention` (lines 64-112)\\n\\nBoth implementations are created through the factory pattern in `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/compactor.go:New()` (lines 55-73), which routes to either periodic or revision-based compaction.\\n\\n### 2. Compaction of Revision Indices\\n\\n**Index Compaction** (`server/storage/mvcc/key_index.go`):\\n- The `Compact()` method on `keyIndex` removes old revisions of keys\\n- Processes the `generations` structure (lines 44-72 in key_index.go comments) which tracks key mutations\\n- `doCompact()` (lines 258-282) walks through key generations and removes revisions <= compactionRev\\n- Maintains `available` map to track which revisions should be kept\\n\\n**Backend Compaction** (`server/storage/mvcc/kvstore_compaction.go:scheduleCompaction`):\\n- Iterates through backend storage in batches (lines 42-99)\\n- Deletes entries with revisions that are not in the `keep` map (generated from index compaction)\\n- Uses configurable batch limits via `CompactionBatchLimit` and sleep intervals via `CompactionSleepInterval`\\n- Records metrics: `indexCompactionPauseMs`, `dbCompactionTotalMs`, `dbCompactionKeysCounter`, `dbCompactionLast`\\n\\n### 3. Notification of Watch Streams Spanning Compacted Revisions\\n\\nWhen a watcher's minimum revision falls below the compaction revision, it must be notified:\\n\\n**Watch Stream Cancellation** (`server/storage/mvcc/watcher_group.go:chooseAll`, lines 237-266):\\n- During sync of unsynced watchers, `chooseAll()` checks if `w.minRev < compactRev`\\n- Sends a `WatchResponse` with `CompactRevision: compactRev` (line 253)\\n- Marks the watcher as `compacted = true` (line 254)\\n- Removes the watcher from the group (line 255)\\n- This notification tells clients their watch window has been compacted away\\n\\n**Watch Synchronization** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go:syncWatchers`, lines 346-414):\\n- Unsynced watchers are synced in batches (maxWatchersPerSync = 512)\\n- Retrieves events from current store state and sends to watchers\\n- Watches that couldn't send due to full channels become \\\"victims\\\" (lines 390-405)\\n- Calls `slowWatcherGauge.Set()` to track slow watchers (line 411)\\n\\n**Victim Handling** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go:moveVictims` and `syncVictimsLoop`, lines 257-339):\\n- Maintains a list of blocked watchers (\\\"victims\\\") that couldn't receive events\\n- Retries sending events to victims every 10ms (line 272)\\n- Once successfully sent, moves watchers back to synced/unsynced groups\\n- Decrements `slowWatcherGauge` when a slow watcher is no longer slow (line 324)\\n\\n### 4. Slow Watch Detection\\n\\nSlow watchers (watchers that fall behind) are tracked and managed:\\n\\n**Metrics** (`server/storage/mvcc/metrics.go`):\\n- `slowWatcherGauge` (lines 87-94): Tracks total number of unsynced slow watchers\\n- `pendingEventsGauge` (lines 105-112): Tracks pending events awaiting delivery\\n- Updated during `syncWatchers()` at line 411 of watchable_store.go\\n\\n**Detection Mechanism** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go`):\\n- When a watcher's channel is full (can't send), it's marked as `victim = true` (line 505)\\n- The slow watcher gauge is incremented (line 508) when moved to unsynced\\n- The gauge is decremented (line 324) when the watcher recovers\\n- Slow watchers are defined as unsynced watchers that haven't caught up to current revision\\n\\n### 5. Integration with Server\\n\\nThe compactor is integrated into the etcd server (`server/etcdserver/server.go`):\\n- Field `compactor v3compactor.Compactor` (line 266) holds the active compactor\\n- Created during server startup with `v3compactor.New()` \\n- Runs in a background goroutine via `srv.compactor.Run()` (line 388)\\n- Stopped via `compactor.Stop()` during graceful shutdown (line 962)\\n\\n### Key Files Summary\\n\\n1. **Compaction Scheduling**: `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/{compactor.go, periodic.go, revision.go}`\\n2. **Compaction Implementation**: `server/storage/mvcc/{kvstore_compaction.go, key_index.go}`\\n3. **Watch Stream Management**: `server/storage/mvcc/{watchable_store.go, watcher_group.go, watcher.go}`\\n4. **Metrics and Monitoring**: `server/storage/mvcc/metrics.go`\\n5. **Server Integration**: `server/etcdserver/server.go`\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
